$.unsubscribe([deferEvent, initTrack]);
espn.track.init(data); } }
if(initOnLoad || window.espn_ui.userParsed){ initTrack(); } else { $.subscribe(deferEvent, initTrack); timeoutID = window.setTimeout(initTrack, 5000); } } );
});
}
